4. ascharyapadiri ento lecina prabhuvun chuci,
Ayanan ghanaparachi stutiyincudi halleluya padudi 
5.sramanondi siluvapai maunamu vahinchenesu,
Ayanan ghanaparaci stutiyinchudi halleluya padudi 
6. Krīstukai sramanonducu sahincumu anniṭini,
Ayanan ghanaparaci stutiyinchudi halleluya padudi 
7.ascharyakarudu pilchen alakinchi rammu vegame,
Adbhutamulanu anubhavinchi padumu halleluya 

Song Number: 868
EN Title: Yee bhuvipai paraloka vinthaina
Pallavi : Yee bhuvipai paraloka vinthaina janamaa,
Prabhu Yesu kristulo thana parishudhulaku,
Jayamitchu devunuki strothramulu.
1. Prabhulo nee prayasam vyartham kaadu,.
Prabhuni panilo yerige yedhuguchunu,
Sthirulai aasakthitho saagudi.
2. Noothana sristi naasinchu meeru,
Sudha pravarthanan prabhu dhrushtiki,
Aagupada jaagrathaga naduvumaa.
3. Kristhu prabhuni prathyaksha mandhu,
Nirapara adhuluga nilabadanu meeru,
Santhito nadapu nanthamu varaku.
4. Dhoshive neevu gathamu dhushtriyalatho,
Nirdhoshiga prabhu sannidhi niluvaabhetta,
Praanamitchi samaadhaana parache.
5. Krishthesu bhandapai kattabadiyu,
Suvaartha sathya nireekshanalu,
Viduvaka viswaasamutho niluvudi.
6. Sathkaryamulannitanu saphaluguchu,
Santhoshimpa prabhu sarvaamulo,
Thandritho naadhuvu thaginatluga.
7. Dhaivaathma suthulu devunni vaarasulu,
Siluva sramalan kreesthu sahavaarasulu,
Mahima pondaga Yesutho mahimalo.

Song Number: 871
EN Title: Gunatisayamula ne padedanu
Pallavi : Gunatisayamula ne padedanu 2
Stuti prasansa ne chesedanu,
Gunatisayamula ne padedanu 2
1.Papa sagaramulo ne munugu cunti,
Na kannitini ne tragucunti,
Nadu hrdayamu bahu vyakula monde 2,
A samayamulo prabhu naku dorike 2.,
Nannadarinci tana yinta cherchenu 2
2.Hrdaya papamulanni kadige raktamuto,
Nitya rajyamunaku palivaniga jese,
Santi anandamuto prabhu nannu nimpenu,
Nitya jiva varamu nakanugrahincenu,
Tana centaku nannu cercenu prabhuvu
3. Tirigi leci prabhu vellenu paramuku,
Sid'dhaparachuchunde nakai sthalamunu,
Nannukoni pova 1 prabhu tirigi vaccunu,
Vidipincunu nannu prati duḥkhamu nundi,
E niriksanato jivincucunnanu.
